 Know all about Indira Gandhi National Center for Arts
 
 
 1
 IGNCA is based in Delhi and is a large art organization in India, where many big artists from all over the world come to exhibit their art
 2
 It was founded in memory of former Prime Minister Indira Gandhi
 3
 It was launched on 19 November 1985 by Rajiv Gandhi during an event
 4
 The foundation of this institution was laid by Kapila Vatsyayan
 5
 The Indira Gandhi National Center for Arts Trust was registered on 24 March 1987
 6
 The purpose of establishing this institution was to promote national unity and consciousness through art
 7
 a variety of research programs, training, publications and creative activities are organized and conducted here at different times

 The petition said that every person has a matter of privacy and any rule should be made by the central government

 On 23 September last year, the Delhi High Court had asked whatsapp to delete the user data till 25 September
 hoicourt kaa kahana tha ki 25 sitambar se pehle agar koi yujar apana acount delit karata he or use fasebuk ke saath saajha nahin karata he to company ko soochna sarwar se delit kerani hogi
 But whatsapp can share the data after September 25 with Facebook

 Before that, whatsapp had changed its policy to share its users' data with Facebook

 The petition has challenged the decision of the Delhi High Court
 haalanki chif justise jees khehar ne yachikakarta se poocha ki ye free sarvice he

 The High Court said that before September 25, if a user deletes his account and does not share it with Facebook, then the company will have to delete it from the information server
 lekin 25 sitambar ke baad ke data ko whatsap, fasebuk ke saath saajha kar saktaa he

" " Cleanest Railway Station Winner: Jodhpur Cause: In 2016, it was ranked 187th among India's railway stations in cleanliness, and today it has achieved the status of the cleanest railway station in India, according to a 2016 survey of railway stations
 Was ranked 187th
 phir 2018 tak uttar-pashchim railway jone kii ranking main sheersh sthaan par aa chukaa tha
 It has now won the India Today Safagiri Award for the cleanest railway station in India
 kul 150 se zyada log dastaanon-mask se las hokar, 27 alag-alag tarah kii mashiinon kii madad se teen shift main kaam karte hai or nirantar stesan ko saaf banaae rakhte hai
 There is also a separate shelter for the cleaning staff to have food and rest in free time
 stesan adhikari unke liye prerit karne vaale abhiyaan bhi chalaate hai
 The station also has 180 dustbin and plastic bottle blasting machines
 is mashin se niklaa 450 kilo kooda ricycling ke liye bheja ja chukaa he
 The station also has a compost pit, which is used to provide manure to the lush green area of the station premises
 *** One newborn baby girl was found in unclaimed condition in Jaipur and Pali district in Rajasthan
 inamen se jaipur ke jagatpura railway stesan par patariyon ke najadik mili samay purv hui navjaat bacchee ne upachaar ke dauraan dam tod diya
 According to JK Lone Hospital Superintendent SD Sharma, the newborn girl found on the tracks at Jagatpura railway station was brought to the hospital by ambulance service 108
 uski haalat atyant najuk hone ke kaaran gahan chikitsa ikai main bhartee karke use bachaane kaa harsambhav prayaas kiya gaya
 According to Sharma, due to the premature birth of a newborn girl, her weight was only seven hundred grams and many organs were not even fully developed
 navjaat bacchee ne shaam ko upachaar dauraan dam tod diya
 The comments idhar, rajkeey railway police sutron kaa kahana he ki jagatpura railway stesan se kuch duuri par navjaat bacchee milane se kuch samay pehle hi agra-ajmer train gujri thi

 Ranveer Singh, who started his acting career with the band Baaja Baaraat in 2010, has achieved the status of a superstar in Bollywood today
 jahaan unki pichhali film padmavat ne 300 karod se upar kii kamai kii, vahiin haalia release simba akele bhartiya bazaar main do sau karod se zyada kaa kaarobaar kar chuki he
 His upcoming film "gully Boy" is also getting tremendous response from the people
 iske baad ve kapil dev kii byopic "83" main nazar aane vaale hai
 There is no doubt that Ranveer is currently the biggest star in the industry
 unki filmon kaa collection is baat kii gavaahi bhi de rahaa he
 But there was also a period in his life when he had forgotten the dream of becoming an actor
 ranvir ne apane ek puraane intervyuu main bataaya bhi he, "bharat main filmon ko puja jaataa he or har javaan ladke ke dil main kahin na kahin hero banane kii khwaahish hoti he
 It is very interesting that actors in India are called actors less and heroes more
 ""main bhi bachapan se hi filmon kii duniya se kaaphi prabhavit tha, bhale hi filmi parivaar se dur kaa sambandh tha, lekin main ek tarah se hindi film industry main bahari hi tha
 In such a situation, i thought that you can get a leading role in a film only if you have a film background or you are a star kid
 ""eemaandaaree se kahuun to 15-16 saal kii umr tak maine apane actor banane ke sapane ko bhula diya tha or main copiriter banane kii taiyaari karne laga
 i moved to the United States to study advertising

 " In Pakistan's southern Sindh province, a bus rammed into an oil tanker killed 32 people, including 11 children, while 20 others were injured
 shanivaar der raat hyderabad shahar ke sameep hui is durghatana ke baad bheeshan aag lag gai, kyonki tanker main 40 hajaar litre eendhan bharaa tha
 Reports suggest that the driver of the oil tanker slept inside the tanker parked on the roadside
 bas ne sadak kinare khadey isi tanker main peeche se takkar de maari
 The bus was carrying about 50 people including children and women
 kshetreey police adhikari mohammad faruk ne ghatnasthal par yah jaankaree di
 Farooq turned to Taya, the driver of the bus lost control and hit the oil tanker from behind
 ghatana main 32 log maare gaye tathaa kai anya ghayal ho gaye
 He said that children and women were among those who died
 kuch shav buree tarah kshat-vikshat ho gaye hai or pahchaan se pare hai
 Relief service officials said that most of the bodies were so burnt that they were not recognized
 faruk ne bataaya ki takkar ke baad donon vaahanon main aag lag gai or adhiktar log jalane se mare
 He said that firefighters were delayed in reaching the spot and people sitting in front of the bus could not get out due to flames

 yah team or koi nahin balki oman kii team he
 Oman has also beaten Ireland on Wednesday, performing brilliantly

 bhartiya mul ke jo paanch khilaadi is team main apni jagah pakki kar chuke hai, ve hai munish ansaari, ajay laalcheta, jatinder singh, rajesh kumaar or vaibhav vaategaonkar
 Munish Ansari was born in Indore and has also been praised by Rahul Dravid and Wasim Akram
 munish net practice ke dauraan sachin tendulkar or andru ko bhi out kar chuke hai

 yah mana jaataa he kii munish 140 se bhi zyada kii raftaar se bowling karte hai

 vah spin bowling bhi kar lete hai

 saurashtra ke under 16, under 19 or under 22 kii team main unhen jagah mil chuki he

 Jatinder Singh is born in Ludhiana
 oman kii team ke vah ek achche ballebaaj hai
 So far, Oman has scored 175 runs at an average of around 18, playing 10 T20 matches for the team
 sirf itnaa nahin is team kaa koching staff bhi bharat kaa hai
 Oman's spin bowling coach is Sunil Joshi
 sunil joshi bharat kii taraf se 15 test or 69 ekadivasiy match khel chuke hai
 In 1999, Sunil Joshi bowled brilliantly against South Africa, taking five wickets for just 6 runs
 sunil joshi hyderabad va jammu-kashmir team ke coach bhi rahe chuke hai
 Vijay Bhardwaj is the fielding coach of the Oman team
 bharadwaj bharat kii taraf se ekadivasiy match khel chuke hai
 Bhardwaj won the "man of the Series" award for his all-round performance in his first series
 bharadwaj karnataka ranjai trophy ke coach bhi rah chuke hai
 The comments pakistan mul ke jo khilaadi is team main hai, ve hai sultan ahamed jo captain hai, khawar ali, zeeshaan siddiqui, bilal khan, adnan illyas or aamir ali
 Sri Lanka's Duleep Mendis Oman is the team's chief batting coach while Ramesh Ratnayake is the pace bowling coach
 mendis or ratnayake srilanka ke liye cricket khel chuke hai
 If you are a team like this oman ne shandaar pradarshan karte hue buudhvaar ko ireland ko bhi haraaya he
 It is the same Ireland that has defeated Pakistan and West Indies in the World Cup
 sirf itnaa hi nahin oman team ke koching staff main bhi zyada se zyada bharat or srilankai mul ke log hai
 The five players of Indian origin who have confirmed their place in this team are Munish Ansari, Ajay Lalcheta, Jatinder Singh, Rajesh Kumar and Vaibhav Wategavkar
 munish ansaari kaa janm indore main hua he or unki tarif rahul dravid or wasim akram bhi kar chuke hai

 laalcheta saurashtra ke liye bhi khel chuke hai
 He has got a place in Saurashtra's Under 16, Under 19 and Under 22 teams
 sirf laalcheta hi nahin rajesh kumaar kaa janm bhi gujarat ke paalan main hua he
